[17-Feb-21 03:41 PM] stacey#1000
(HOTEL RULES)

You will now be given mod at the hotel with the ability to kick anyone that commits a major offence or trollers with 3 warnings.

Major offences:

-Bypassing the chat filter
-Major spamming
-Inappropriate attire 
-Inappropriate/ offensive username 
-Exploiting
-Major trolling (kicked 3+ times)
-Glitching repeatedly
-Discrimination 


Like as an LR, you will need to report it in one of the reports channels in the Bloxton discord then kick the user.

For trollers with 3 warnings, you must check chatlogs to ensure the user actually has 3 warnings before kicking them. There can be cases where the user has false warnings or does not have 3 warnings at all, that is why you must check to ensure they have 3 valid warnings. 

If they have 3 valid warnings, you may kick the troller for 3 warnings.

Abusing staff members: You will find staff members abusing at the hotel, it is a given. If you're in that situation, go to the staff discussion channel via the Bloxton discord and request for a rank 11+. If an HR is online, provide the proof and username of the abuser on the staff discussion channel and ping them. Be sure to be respectful when pinging!

If a security is abusing handcuffs you may remove their tools or respawn them. 

Commands you can use at the hotel:

Be sure to NOT abuse at the hotel. This can and will get you fired. However, there are multiple commands you can use to your advantage.

Appropriate commands:

-view
-bring (i.e if someone is glitched or a troller is running)
-to
-kick
